City Public Security Bureau: Secret Arrest of Four Communists on Orders - Xie Zuoyu and Three Others Arrested at No. 45 Continental New Village - Xie Holds Master's Degrees from Harvard and Cornell Universities, Chen is a College Student - Lawyers Argue Over Evidence During Transfer to High Court Branch - Police Lawyer Believes Xie and Others Have No Counter-Revolutionary Suspicions and Should Be Released 160

—Result: Adjournment Pending Submission of Conclusive Evidence by the City Public Security Bureau; Xie and Others Released on Bail Pending Trial—

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau's Supervisory Department recently received a secret order stating that communists were hiding at No. 45 Continental New Village, Shikota Road in northern Shanghai. The department investigated and determined that Continental New Village was located on an extraterritorial road. At 10:55 AM, they coordinated with detectives from the Fifth District Police Station and rushed to make the arrests. At that time, two Indian police officers from the Wayside Road Police Station were patrolling the area. Believing that the area was under the jurisdiction of the concession, they reported the matter to the police station via telephone. The police station immediately ordered Chinese detective Tan Jinhai and foreign detective Witte to go and prevent unilateral arrest. Together, they arrested four people inside the house: Chen Yuxiu and Xie Xinming from Guangdong, Xie Zuoyu, and Xu Jian from Suzhou. Books and manuscripts were seized and taken back to the police station. It was discovered that Chen and others were graduates of Soochow University, while Xie Zuoyu held master's degrees from Harvard and Cornell Universities in the United States. He had been doing business in Southeast Asia and had recently arrived in Shanghai less than two months ago. He was temporarily detained. Yesterday afternoon, they were transferred to the Criminal Division of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Judge Zhou Han opened the court for investigation. Police representatives lawyers Li Zhishan and Gan Jingxian, and James K.F. Chang the legal advisor to the Public Security Bureau, were also present in court. First, Police Lawyer Li stated that the police had found that the four defendants had no criminal suspicion. The "kerosene" books that the Public Security Bureau considered evidence were also deemed to have no counter-revolutionary content. Therefore, he requested that the Public Security Bureau provide sufficient evidence before agreeing to the transfer. Otherwise, he requested that the defendants be released on bail, as the police had originally intended to release the defendants. When questioned, the defendants all denied joining any party or organization. Chen Ming, a supervisor from the City Public Security Bureau, stated that this was a secret order and that the defendants were important figures in the Territory Guarantee League in the French Concession, which was a communist organization. Lawyer James K.F. Chang immediately stated that the case was of great importance and requested permission to transfer the defendants. Police Lawyer Li Zhishan immediately responded that the Public Security Bureau had not provided sufficient evidence and could not conclusively prove that the defendants were communists, only stating that it was a secret order. Such baseless accusations and arrests violated the legal protection of the people and should be noted by the court. Lawyer James K.F. Chang then requested the court to adjourn the case for one week to allow the Public Security Bureau to collect evidence and submit it. Lawyer Li Zhishan added that the police believed that the defendants had no counter-revolutionary suspicion and had wanted to release them at the time of the arrest. As a precautionary measure, they were temporarily detained. Now that the Public Security Bureau was requesting an adjournment, it was still uncertain whether they would be able to present conclusive evidence in the future. To avoid the imprisonment of innocent people and maintain the people's right to protection, he requested that the defendants be released on bail. Lawyer James K.F. Chang opposed this request. Judge Zhou then ruled that the case be adjourned for further hearing, and the four defendants were released on bail of 500 yuan each. Hearing this, Lawyer James K.F. Chang made a statement regarding the bail, stating that the circumstances of the case were extremely serious. If the defendants were only required to pay 500 yuan bail and were to escape in the future, who would be responsible? He requested the court to consider this. Judge Zhou declared that the Public Security Bureau did not have sufficient evidence today. After considering the case, the court decided to release the defendants on bail. The purpose of bail was to prevent escape. If they were to escape, the guarantor would be held responsible. Since the evidence was insufficient today, the 500 yuan bail was deemed appropriate. As for what would happen in the future, it could not be predicted. Therefore, the court believed there was nothing inappropriate. After finishing his statement, he adjourned the court.

British Mrs. Hartley: Sentenced to Hang for Murdering Her Lover 161

Mrs. Hartley, a British woman of Russian descent, was sentenced to hang by British Acting Judge Jones the other day for murdering her lover, Youngers. The execution will be carried out once it is approved by the British Minister to China. According to the law, the woman still has the right to appeal, but since she is penniless, it is unlikely that she will be able to appeal. Another glimmer of hope is a pardon or reduction of sentence from the British Minister. However, given the circumstances of the case, the hope of a pardon is slim. If the sentence is carried out, it would be unprecedented for a British woman residing in the Far East to be executed. Therefore, the case has attracted much attention from foreigners during the repeated hearings, and the visitor's gallery has always been full. After the interrogation was completed the other afternoon, the twelve jurors retired to the secret chamber for an hour and a quarter before returning to court and declaring the defendant guilty but requesting the court to show mercy. Judge Jones then declared the murder charge established and sentenced the defendant to death by hanging according to law. This case occurred on the evening of August 16th at No. 17, Lane 166, Mao Hai Road. The two had been living together for less than a month. Neighbors saw the woman stabbing Youngers and reported it to the police, who broke into the house and found Youngers lying in a pool of blood, already dead. His neck had been stabbed with a kitchen knife, penetrating more than five inches. The woman was lying in the inner room, disheveled and drunk. She was taken back to the police station and sent to the British Concession Court for interrogation, and the verdict was reached the other day. The woman was a middle-aged widow. Nine years ago, she became acquainted with Youngers, a British man who had worked as a shipowner. However, their relationship was marked by periods of intense affection and periods of conflict and separation. They lived together several times, drifting in and out of each other's lives like duckweed on water. Recently, she had fallen into prostitution and was rescued by a foreign relief organization. She then rekindled her old romance with Youngers, but tragically, it ended in violence.

When questioned, he was unable to speak and was wearing Japanese clothing, so he was identified as Japanese. He was hired a car and sent to Fumin Hospital. It was later learned that he was a Cantonese man named Liang Di, who was then transferred to the police station hospital for treatment. After the fire was extinguished, a large quantity of morphine powder for manufacturing heroin and a large pot of unfinished heroin material, as well as chemical machinery and other items, were found inside the premises. The police then discovered that the premises were a large-scale heroin manufacturing operation, established by the Japanese national Nagasawa. He was arrested and sent to the Japanese consulate for legal punishment. The Cantonese man Liang Di remained in a coma in the hospital, refusing to speak. The police were unable to determine who had hired him and could only file a report under the name Liang Di, age and surname unknown. They submitted the case to the First Special District Court, pending his recovery for questioning. It was not until the other day that he suddenly spoke, claiming that he was from Chaozhou, named Xiao Zhifen, only seventeen years old, and worked as a general affairs officer for a Japanese man at the premises. He had recently come to Shanghai from his hometown and did not know anything else. Yesterday morning, the police corrected his name and sent him to the Third Criminal Court. Lawyer Zhang Tianyin presented the case, stating that the owner of the premises, Japanese national Nagasawa (i.e., Nagasawa), had been sentenced to one month's imprisonment by the Japanese consulate. He was present in court to testify. He presented the previously seized evidence, heroin, a pot of unfinished raw materials, and photographs of various machines for inspection. He stated that the material had been chemically tested by a Public Works Department doctor and confirmed to be the chemical juice for manufacturing heroin. The defendant's claim of living downstairs was false. Firefighters could testify that he had jumped from upstairs. They were also present in court. According to Nagasawa's testimony, he was a car dealer. He rented the premises in October of last year. He lived downstairs with his wife and two Chinese men and one Chinese woman, who were all servants. The upstairs was sublet to a Cantonese man named Li. The heroin materials and other items seized were all owned by the man surnamed Li, and the defendant was hired by him and was not his general affairs officer. Then, Li Defu, a Korean firefighter, testified that the defendant jumped from the balcony upstairs, fell unconscious to the ground, and was helped up by him. He was unable to speak at that time, so he was taken to the hospital by car. When questioned, the defendant spoke Chaozhou dialect, and there was no translator. The police lawyer asked him to speak some Shanghainese, and he replied that he came to Shanghai from Chaozhou only two months ago and worked as a general affairs officer for a Japanese man at the premises. He lived downstairs, and the upstairs was occupied by a Chinese man named Wang Hongsheng. He did not know what the latter was doing. When the fire broke out, he was sleeping soundly downstairs, woke up in alarm, and fell to the ground while escaping. The court asked if the Japanese man at his house was Nagasawa. After observing him, he said it was not him. His other testimony was evasive. Nagasawa stated that there was no other Japanese man at his place. His testimony was inaccurate, and there was no Chinese man named Wang Hongsheng. The police lawyer Zhang stated that the premises were indeed a large-scale heroin manufacturing operation. Another Cantonese man was still at large. Who established the organization was important to international relations. He requested another extension to investigate whether the defendant was the general affairs officer at the premises or an assistant in the organization. Judge Xiao Xiefen ordered that the case be adjourned for further review. The next time the court convened, the police were instructed to bring a Chaozhou translator to clarify the truth.

Notice from the French Concession Police Department: The French Concession Police Department is searching for a Chinese man who, on the evening of October 15th at approximately 11:00 PM, was involved in a case at No. 12 Hengqing Lane, Beile Road in the French Concession, in which a French Police Department foreign detective and a Public Security Bureau detective were brutally murdered. If anyone can provide information about the above person that leads to his arrest, the Police Department will offer a significant reward. Meeting of the Cotton Traders Association - Telegram to Minister Song Requesting Assistance 166

Yesterday afternoon at 7:00 PM, the Shanghai Cotton Traders Association held its 14th Executive Committee meeting. More than ten people attended, including Zhou Kai, Tang Qixian, Zhou Chunbo, Zhu Jinsheng, Zhou Bocun, Yang Yanbo, and Wu Jiliu. Ding Yutian was elected temporary chairman. The meeting was conducted according to protocol. The recording report was abbreviated. Discussion and resolutions: (1) Cotton procurement case. Resolution: Send letters to cotton procurement offices in Hankou and Shashi, requesting that the cotton be pure to preserve the industry's reputation. Passed. (2) The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's warehouse proposed rent starting after half a month for cotton imported from Shashi. Resolution: Send a letter to the General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, requesting that cotton imported from Shashi be treated the same as cotton from Hankou. Passed. (3) Cotton loan case. Resolution: Send a telegram to Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance requesting that he use stopgap and fundamental measures to help the cotton industry, traders, and farmers. Passed. The meeting adjourned at 8:30 PM. The telegram to Minister Song is recorded below. To Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: Since the cotton and wheat loan was finalized, the government has established the National Economic Commission, with you, Minister, being specially selected to oversee its functions. You are using a unified system to restore rural areas, regulate food, silk, tea, cotton, and mining to resist foreign economic aggression and to take overall planning into account, for the benefit of the whole country. Recently, you have also initiated the Unified Cotton Industry Committee, recruiting specialized personnel to create a sound organization. Looking at the declaration, from expanding cotton fields, improving planting, increasing textiles, and regulating labor and capital, everything is planned and detailed, and thoroughly considered. All of us in the cotton industry admire you greatly. In every country, social reforms are preceded by hardship, and only then can we achieve lasting benefits. This is a necessary path. If the medicine does not cause dizziness, the illness will not be cured. The people of the country also know that without the determination to be firm and patient and to work hard with the government, it will not be possible to lay a foundation that will last for centuries. However, since the national crisis, the market has been depressed, rural areas have gone bankrupt, and the people's suffering is indescribable. Just in the cotton industry alone, with the dumping of foreign goods and the general economic recession, the national cotton industry has already plummeted. When news of the arrival of American cotton came, prices fell sharply again. The average cotton trader and farmer are aware that the government's cotton and wheat loan has a far-reaching plan for the national economy. However, the current impact has put the cotton traders and farmers at risk of collapse. Furthermore, when national cotton is harvested, American cotton is arriving. Since the government has announced that American cotton will not be sold to Japan, then all American cotton and national cotton must be consumed in the domestic market. Supply exceeds demand, and prices will inevitably fall. It can be concluded that production will increase daily, while demand will decrease. At the same time, foreign goods continue to be dumped. The future situation may be even worse than it is today. If the government does not take measures to assist in advance, the exhausted cotton traders and farmers will not be able to survive. Abandoning the root and pursuing the branch is a poor strategy. It seems that both stopgap and fundamental measures should be implemented. It is believed that there are approximately two aspects to the stopgap measures: (1) Stabilize market prices. Currently, as cotton prices are declining, not only are traders suffering losses, but also planters will not be able to support themselves. The government should investigate the situation and find ways to stabilize cotton market prices to reduce losses for both traders and farmers and to maintain the status quo. (2) Improve dyeing and weaving. Domestically produced cotton fabrics, especially floral-labeled cloth, are the most sold. Since the European War, Japan has shipped more than 100 million units of floral-labeled cloth to our country each year. The amount shipped by European and American countries is also not small. In the past two years, although the import of Japanese goods has decreased, the import of Russian goods has increased sharply. The actual outflow of money remains the same. If our country's cotton industry does not improve dyeing and weaving, but relies solely on increasing spindles and expanding native cloth looms, it may lead to a tragic situation of product stagnation and textile factory shutdowns. The plan for now is to first investigate the domestic sales of floral-labeled cloth and native cloth, and immediately promote floral-labeled cloth dyeing and weaving factories. If the resources are insufficient, the government should provide subsidies to ensure that the products meet the needs and do not stagnate. The government should take the lead above, and the people should create and manufacture below. In this way, loopholes can be plugged, and domestic products can circulate. By addressing both the symptoms and the root causes, both the national economy and people's livelihood will benefit. We respectfully submit this telegram for your review and approval for implementation. This will be fortunate for the country and fortunate for the cotton industry. Shanghai Cotton Traders Association kowtows, Hao.

Yi Peiji Discusses the Case of Ancient Artifacts from the Palace Museum: Forced to Counter-Sue; Handover of Palace Museum Affairs Completed 169

Following the counter-suit filed by former Palace Museum Director Yi Peiji, the general public has paid close attention. Yesterday, a person close to Yi visited him at the French-operated Qiyi Hospital. The following is a record of the conversation: Q: What brings you to Shanghai? A: I have suffered from diabetes for several years, and it has recently worsened, so I came to Shanghai for treatment. Also, Cui Zhenhua and Zou Lie colluded to frame me, and I also want to come south to appeal. Q: The Palace Museum lawsuit has been going on for months, why haven't you appeared in court? A: This matter came to light on May 1st of this year. On that day, the Supreme Procuratorate sent prosecutor Zhu Shusheng to Beijing to interrogate me. I personally appeared in court for questioning, which lasted for four hours. Afterwards, Zhu repeatedly summoned Li Zongtong and others for questioning. Each time, they had to go to the Beijing District Court, which is documented. How can you say I didn't appear in court? Upon discovering the telegram of Zou Lie's illegal arrest, there were also rumors of imprisoning us and handing us over to Puyi (because the ancient artifacts of the Palace Museum, along with the ancestral tablet of Qing Taizu and portraits of Puyi's ancestors, were all being transported. This was tantamount to capturing Puyi, and he hated me to the core). Moreover, since the legal power was in the hands of the other party, if I surrendered myself, I would not only be left to the enemy, but also be subjected to illegal imprisonment. As an old and sickly man, how could I endure such suffering in the scorching heat of summer? I feared that by the time I was declared innocent, I would have already died in prison. The reason I didn't appear in court afterwards is all due to these kinds of hardships. Q: Then why didn't you counter-sue? A: There were also difficulties. Puyi and I have been friends for over ten years, and we were also old members of the Republican Party. If we were to sue each other, it would give others something to criticize. The Supreme Court judge openly bribed and exposed corruption, which would affect the country's image. Therefore, I endured humiliation and waited for the other party to come to their senses. This is why I didn't want to file a counter-suit hastily. Q: What was the handover situation like? A: The Beijing Palace Museum's general affairs office, such as general affairs accounting, security guards, and document departments, the secretariat's documents and files, have all been handed over clearly. The receiving committee members have all stamped and signed. The important artifacts have been transported to Shanghai and are being inventoried. Q: Are there any problems during the inventory? A: I have heard that the other party has plans to create incidents during the inventory of artifacts, use news tactics, and promote social gossip to use as weapons in the lawsuit. Everyone knows that the Palace Museum has no corruption. Even if some of the boxes are overturned when they are opened, it is understandable during the hectic rush of transportation. Moreover, the packing and custodian staff are directly responsible, and all of them are still on duty. There is no way to follow Zheng Lie's method of investigating them.

Knitted Goods Shipped to Hangzhou for Sale Must Have Proof from the National Products Association Because Non-Domestic Raw Materials are Being Used to Counterfeit Brands for Dumping 170

The China National Products Maintenance Association recently received a letter from the Hangzhou Knitted Goods Industry Association, stating: Dear Sirs, Upon investigation, since the September 18th Incident, all Japanese goods have been dumped at reduced prices as part of Japan's economic aggression. Some unscrupulous merchants, seeking only profit, disregard the national interest, resulting in the daily promotion of national products by the people, while customs records show that the import of Japanese goods has increased daily. National product manufacturers have made no progress, and the consequences of this situation are unbearable. To correct this, a fundamental solution is needed. According to reports, ten factories in Shanghai, including Gongzu, Sanyang, Jiuyi, Dingxin, Yutai, Junchang, Yingzhou, Yongyuan, Yixing, and Tonghe, are using inferior Japanese Limabrand yarn to replace it with domestic Zhongsha yarn. As a result, the finished products are sold to the interior as national products, which in reality means that inferior goods are occupying the market and defeating genuine national products. The association's temporary members' meeting has resolved that all such goods will be refused entry in the future. All goods shipped from Shanghai to Hangzhou by the industry must have proof from the China National Products Maintenance Association, along with the unified tax form, in order to be sold in the market, thereby maintaining national products and preventing genuine domestic manufacturers from being driven to ruin. We are writing to your association to ask you to investigate and handle this matter, and to provide a list of the factory brands in Shanghai that are confirmed to be using domestic raw materials, so that we can inform our colleagues. Thank you for your cooperation. Upon receiving this letter, the association has investigated and implemented the matter cautiously.

Shanghai Savings and Remittance Bureau Abolished; Business Handled by the General Bureau; Name Abolished by Year-End 171

Nanjing, 19th (Central News Agency) - The issue of the Postal Savings and Remittance General Bureau being transferred to the Postal General Bureau was submitted by the Executive Yuan to the Central Political Committee for decision. The principle was to be implemented by the Ministry. However, the review of the relevant laws and regulations required time. In order to conserve and tighten resources, the Ministry ordered the Postal Savings and Remittance General Bureau to abolish the Shanghai Savings and Remittance Bureau, with business handled by the General Bureau. City Chamber of Commerce Writes to the Public Works Department to Correct the Current Policy of the Electricity Company: Using the Employer System to Control Laborers; Perpetual Harmony Cannot Be Expected 172

The City Chamber of Commerce wrote to the Public Works Department yesterday: Dear Sirs, Since the workers of the Shanghai Electric Power Company's new factory went on strike due to the company's continuous dismissals and refusal to pay pensions, the company has locked the factory gates and refused workers entry, leading to an escalation of the turmoil. The standoff has lasted for more than twenty days. It is understood that labor strikes are a common phenomenon after the development of mechanical industry. However, the solution is nothing more than equal negotiations between labor and management, or impartial mediation by a third party. This is not only the case in advanced industrial countries, but also in Shanghai's Chinese-owned factories when they encounter labor strikes. The Electric Power Company, since it operates within China, cannot disregard this common practice. However, due to its foreign nationality, the company is unwilling to adopt negotiation or mediation procedures, but purely wants to use its employer system to control laborers and force them to submit, as if the methods used by civilized countries to resolve labor strikes are not applicable in the Far East. This kind of anachronistic mentality, even if the policy is effective for a time, cannot be expected to achieve perpetual harmony. Our association hopes that your bureau can use its supervisory position to admonish and correct the current policy of the company.

Pilot License Dispute: Navigation Association Submits Report on the Process to the Ministry 173

The pilots Wang Shaoqing, Wang Maoqing, Fu Xietang, Chen Haishan, Xiang Nengxing, and Zhu Jingan of the Minsheng Industrial Company's three ships, Min Gui, Min Xian, and Min Kang, applied for long-term practice certificates in accordance with regulations, but were obstructed by the Songhu Pilot Association. After repeated unsuccessful negotiations, the Shanghai Navigation Industry Association submitted a report to the Ministry of Communications yesterday: Regarding the submission of a request to the Ministry of the Navy to order the Songhu Pilot Association to submit the conditions for revising the regulations, so that they can be forwarded for understanding. Previously, the association received a telegram requesting immediate assistance because the Songhu Pilot Association was obstructing the transfer of certificates to the long-term pilots Wang Shaoqing and others employed by member Minsheng Industrial Company. The Ministry replied with No. 2075, approving the Navy's consultation on the matter of pilot Wang Shaoqing and others applying for licenses. It was found that the Pilot Training Institute had already issued these certificates and handed them over to the Songhu Pilot Association for forwarding. The institute has stated that due to the business relationship of Wang Shaoqing and others, the association must revise the regulations and the association and the pilots should negotiate on their own. The association should immediately order the completion of the procedures in accordance with regulations and promptly obtain the certificates. This was duly noted, and Minsheng Company was notified to forward it to the pilots. The company replied that the Ministry's approval was noted. The certificates of Wang Shaoqing and others have been issued by the Training Institute, which proves that the procedures have been completed. The fact that the Pilot Association has not followed through also proves that it intends to make things difficult. Other Chinese companies, such as China Merchants, Sanbei, NingShao, etc., and foreign companies, such as Taikoo, Jardine, and Xiangtai, etc., all have their long-term pilots' certificates issued by the Training Institute and forwarded by the association, but there has never been a precedent for revising the regulations. This is the first point. Also, according to the association's articles of association submitted to the Navy for record, there is no provision that any member must revise the regulations. This is the second point. The so-called revising the regulations has no precedent and no basis in the articles of association. It is a superfluous issue and has other intentions, which can be ignored. However, with the company's peace of mind as the premise, the pilots were ordered to compromise and inquire reluctantly. Unexpectedly, the association did not sincerely inform them, so the conditions were unknown and could not be revised. This is regrettable. The pilot association's regulations have all been submitted to the Navy for record, so the conditions that should be revised must also be submitted to the Ministry for record, in order to be solemn and for public use. The Navy should be asked to consult each item and indicate them, so that they can be negotiated. If they have not been submitted for record, the Navy should be asked to order them to report. It should be asked that the association forward the detailed conditions for revising the regulations with pilots Wang Shaoqing and others to the Navy for consultation with the Ministry of Communications, which will order the association to inform the association and inform the pilots for consideration and decision. The association replied that the request was pertinent and reasonable, and it should be forwarded accordingly, requesting approval and consultation for a speedy resolution.

Seventh District Office of Wusong Investigates Case of Trafficked Women 174

Chen Xiaoxing and Li Faping, patrol officers from the 9th outpost of the 7th District of the Wusong Branch Security Bureau, found two suspicious-looking individuals, a man and a woman named Lu Dabao, at the train station yesterday afternoon at 2 PM. They were immediately taken to the district office and interrogated by District Chief Gong. Lu Dabao claimed to be 19 years old, from Yancheng, and had been in Shanghai for four years, working at the Shunxing Factory in Caojiadu. Zhao Xiaoying introduced her to the job. On the 8th of this month, Xiaoying told her not to work at the factory and that her brother would introduce her to a job in Wusong. On the morning of the 9th, she went to a hotel with Zhao Guigang. The next day, they stayed at his friend's house. Then they took a train to Wusong and stayed at his sister's house in Taixing Temple. Today, he ordered her to go to Jiangbei with the intention of marrying her, but she was unwilling because she had been deceived by him. Zhao Guigang confessed that he was 26 years old, from Taizhou, and currently unemployed. He had known Lu Dabao for more than a month. The previous week, some women mentioned that a young woman was unemployed and asked him to introduce her to a job in Wusong. He agreed and took her out. That day, he had her stay in a hotel, while he stayed in Xiaobeimen. The next day, they went to Wusong and stayed at the house of a person named Shi in Taixing Temple for seven days. Because they could not get a job at the Wing On Textile Factory, he intended to send her back to Caojiadu today. District Chief Gong considered this case to involve the trafficking of women from respectable families and ordered that the man and woman be transferred to the General Bureau for punishment.

Tax Collection Office Issues Notice: Strict Prohibition of Impersonation and Multiple Use of Permits 176

The Shanghai Tax Collection Office issued a notice yesterday regarding the strict prohibition of impersonation: It is known that the practice of impersonating and using one permit for multiple transactions has always been prohibited. If such misconduct is discovered, it will be punished according to the regulations to deter others from following suit. It is known that most of the brokers in various districts of the city and county conduct legitimate transactions with registered names and license numbers, but there are also quite a few who impersonate and use one permit for multiple transactions. Such arbitrary and irregular conduct is disrupting the tax regulations and violating the prohibitions. The office should punish the offenders according to their names, but out of consideration that the brokers may not be aware of the violations of the tax regulations, they must be warned again and again. Therefore, a notice is hereby issued to all brokers that impersonation and multiple use of permits are prohibited. They should come to the office to pay taxes and obtain permits as soon as possible, and not wait and see, lest they be investigated and bring trouble upon themselves. After this notice, if there are any more of the above-mentioned misconducts, they will be severely punished and will not be tolerated.

Taikoo Steamship Company's Shengjing Vessel Now Stops at Weihaiwei, in Addition to Dalian and Qingdao 177

The Northern Line (i.e., the Shanghai to Qingdao route) has always been operated by Japanese ships, which are better than both Chinese and British ships. The reason is that the ships are well-equipped and very fast, so they are popular with passengers. In order to maintain navigation rights and for the convenience of passengers, the China Merchants Bureau leased the Puan vessel from the Ministry of the Navy in early summer of this year. For several months, passengers have found it convenient and business has been good. The bureau originally intended to stop the service in the autumn, but due to the requests of merchants in the port, it is continuing to operate. The British company Taikoo Steamship Company has several vessels calling at the port, but because they are mostly cargo ships, they are not suitable for passengers. In order to facilitate passengers, it is reported that the Shengjing vessel on the Northern Line will now stop at Weihaiwei, in addition to Qingdao and Yantai, starting tomorrow, the 21st. Passengers and cargo to Qingdao from Shanghai will not be delayed, and the schedule for Yantai and Tianjin will remain unchanged.

Tenants of Peifuli in Rue du Consulat General Object to Signing New Leases; Mass Meeting Held Yesterday to Discuss Countermeasures 178

There are forty or fifty houses in Peifuli, Rue du Consulat General, in the French Concession. The landlord has always been Peifu Company. Since the company transferred the lease management rights to the Teepock Real Estate Department in April last year, the department issued a notice to the tenants in September of this year, requiring all to sign new leases. The tenants believe that there has never been such a procedure since they rented the houses, and since the real estate department took over, all the tenants have paid rent and there has been no arrears. It is difficult to accept the new leases with their harsh conditions. Therefore, they jointly wrote to the real estate department to express their unanimous opposition. Record of the Annual Meeting of the International Chess Association 179

The Shanghai International Chess Association, which was founded in 1903, held its 30th annual meeting last night on the second floor of the Western YMCA.

This year has the largest number of members, including three female members. It is planned to hold practice sessions every Wednesday and Friday evening. Victoria Nurses' Home Scheduled to Open October 23rd 180

The Victoria Nurses' Home, built by the Public Works Department next to the Hong En Hospital on the Avenue Haig, has been completed and is scheduled to hold an opening ceremony by the board of directors at 4:30 PM next Monday, October 23rd, welcoming the public to participate and visit. It is known that the Victoria Nurses' Home was originally built in 1901 with public donations on the Public Works Department's land on Avenue Road, to commemorate the 50th anniversary of Queen Victoria's accession to the throne. In January 1928, the Public Works Department decided to close the home based on the report of the Economy Committee and decided to rebuild a new home at the current site. The new home is an eight-story building made of steel, concrete, etc., and the exterior is tiled with dark red tiles. The first floor is the kitchen and cold storage room, all with the latest equipment. The second floor is a public hall, accessible by a wide staircase from the main entrance on the Avenue Haig, with a dining room and library, etc. The third to seventh floors are the nurses' residences, all single rooms with south-facing balconies overlooking the garden.

Ms. Chen Mingzhu Opens Clinic to Serve the Public 181

Ms. Chen Mingzhu, the niece of the revolutionary pioneer Chen Qubing, is skilled in medicine, especially obstetrics. She has served in the Wu Men Su Family Hospital for many years and founded the Tongli Hospital. During the Qi-Lu War, she personally went to the war zone to provide medical services. During the January 28th Incident when the Japanese attacked Shanghai, she participated in the Women's Comfort the Soldiers Association with Mrs. Xu Qian and was responsible for ambulance work. Recently, she and Ms. Wang Zhu jointly opened an obstetrics clinic at No. 406 Julaida Road, which is a blessing for women in Shanghai.

Summary of Re-elections of Occupational Unions 182

Newspaper Delivery Industry: The Occupational Union convened a general meeting of all member representatives at 3:00 PM on the 16th of this month to hold the second re-election of the board of directors and supervisors. A total of 93 member representatives attended. There were 21 sitting members and supervisors. Xu Wenrong, Li Linsheng, and Xu Rongxiang were elected as the presidium. Mei Guozhen was the emcee. Feng Zhiyou was the meeting recorder. Li Weixiong, the representative of the City Party Department, attended to provide guidance. Lan Simian, the representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, attended to supervise. The meeting proceeded as scheduled. The chairman reported the purpose of the meeting. The sitting directors, supervisors, secretaries, staff, accountants, and other staff members reported on the work of the association. Then the election began. The election tickets were examined by representatives from the superior agencies, and Xu Rongxiang and Zhao Hongqing were publicly elected to count the votes, Wang Xingying and Lu Xiapu to read the votes, and Ding Changliang and Wu Yuesheng to record the votes. As a result, nine directors were elected: Xu Rongxiang, Zhai Xiaohui, Xu Zhiqin, Xu Wenrong, Tang Gengquan, Yin Yinmu, Zhao Hong, Wang Guisheng, Duan Shoulian. Four alternate directors were elected: Wu Yuesheng, Ding Shunfa, Peng Genrong, Jiang Laiyun. Five supervisors were elected: Chen Ruliang, Dong Wenxuan, Zhang Sanmao, Song Tusheng, Ding Changliang. Two alternate supervisors were elected: Ying Shaoqing, Lin Falian. Due to time constraints, the inauguration ceremony will be held at a later date. It is scheduled to convene all directors, alternate directors, supervisors, and alternate supervisors at 3:00 PM on October 21st to hold an oath-taking ceremony. It was also decided that before the new directors and supervisors take office, all documents will be handled by the secretary of the association. The speech of the superior representative was lengthy and will not be recorded here. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Weather Report 186

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that central China and the surrounding areas will be sunny and cold. The hurricane has turned northeast and is heading north, with a tendency to quickly turn northeast and blow past the south of Kyushu. There will be cyclone rain between Okinawa and Kyushu, and it will also affect the southern coast of Japan at night. There will be tight northern or northwestern winds on the coast and the Yellow Sea in this area. The center of the hurricane was at 2:00 PM within 60 miles of the intersection of 27 degrees north latitude and 126 degrees 30 minutes east longitude, with strong winds. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this city was a high of 75.9 and a low of 56.7. On the same day last year, the high was 62.8 and the low was 52.3.

Letter 187

According to Shen Yongjun, after reading the Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, and Shishi Xinbao of the 17th of this month, each published a news item about a lawsuit involving me and the Great Eastern Dancing Queen, Mei Zhen. The content is completely inconsistent with the facts. I came to Shanghai this spring to study and there is no truth to the fact that I was engaged to the dancer or that I sent her living expenses monthly. Although the dancer once seduced me, I broke off contact with her early because of my eagerness to study. Furthermore, the newspaper's claim that my father owns various businesses and has family property of five or six hundred thousand yuan is also untrue. It is obvious that the other party is coveting my property and deliberately exaggerating in order to achieve their purpose of extortion. It is also claimed that I do not stay at home and often go to dance halls and singing stages, which is slanderous of my reputation and credit. Please correct the report. Respectfully submitted to the Chief Editor of the Shen Bao, Attorney Yin Shijie, October 19th.

▲ Endless Troubles for Shanghai Team

Guangdong's Five Forwards Extremely Active

Shanghai, facing headwind, held its ground. Guangdong's five forwards, taking advantage of the wind, actively attacked. Center forward Li Hongqing, with lightning speed, charged straight into the central army tent. Li Jiangshan was in a hurry to rescue, Li Chuanqiu and Ye Beihua, Ye Qi, were caught squarely by Zhou, the iron gate. Mai Su and Hu Tianbao surrounded Zhou on all sides, unable to move. He gently pushed the ball out of bounds, forcing a corner kick. It was just five minutes from the kickoff when Yang Shuiyi took the kick. The landing point was excellent. Mai Su caught up with a kick, as fast as a bullet. Jiangshan's back served as a rattan shield. With a bang, it bounced far away and was caught up by Ye Beihua, who kicked it again, but it was still caught by the iron gate. The Shanghai formation was a chaotic mess, killing people and horses. In these fifteen minutes, the Shanghai formation was constantly living in a stormy sea.

▲ Shanghai Forwards Muster Courage to Probe

Too Hasty, Good Opportunities Repeatedly Missed

While the Shanghai five forwards resisted desperately, they still sought opportunities to attack. Once, Zhong Yongsen got the ball and passed it over the center back line to Li Yichen. Li passed it to Sun Jinshun. Sun's attack missed, and the ball went out of bounds to the left, losing the opportunity. After seventeen minutes, Shanghai was penalized for two more corner kicks. They were picked up to the center of the goal, but were ultimately saved by the efforts of Jiangshan and Li Ning. After nineteen minutes, Liang Shutang was penalized for a foul. Mai Su took the kick, but the ball was too high and went over the net, missing by a few points. Otherwise, Zhou, the iron gate, would have been powerless. After twenty minutes, Chen Jiaqiu dribbled straight in and passed it to Zhong Yongsen. At this time, the Guangdong defense was empty. Anxious to score, he raised his foot to shoot, but used too much force and missed again. After twenty-two minutes, Guangdong's Hu Tianbao passed the ball to Mai Su, who penetrated deep into the abdomen. Fortunately, Li Ning arrived and desperately saved it, but it was still intercepted by Li Hongqing, who attacked again. The iron gate fumbled while catching the ball due to the strong wind, forcing another corner kick. Yang Shuiyi took the kick, and Jiangshan retaliated with a big kick. The ball then flew into the Guangdong formation, and soon flew to the Shanghai side again. The fierce battle was extremely intense.

▲ Zhou, the Iron Gate, in Great Form

Guangdong's Fierce Generals Unable to Cross the Forbidden Zone

After thirty-two minutes, Guangdong used a short-range passing technique to penetrate the abdomen. Hu Tianbao lifted a foot, and Zhou Xianyan made a beautiful dive save. Shanghai launched a major counterattack again. Sun Jinshun bravely killed the enemy. Fortunately, Li Tiansheng killed from mid-air and angled it out of bounds. The two teams fought a chaotic battle. The iron gate was careful, constantly telling Xiao Jiang not to stray too far. By the end of the first half, it was 0-0, with neither side winning. The ball came and went suddenly, making Chen Quxiang's legs suffer, running non-stop was the most difficult task. During the break, Shanghai's leader Yu Hengzhi gave instructions. Guangdong's coaches also gathered their athletes and whispered privately. In the second half, they switched sides. Shanghai was downwind, and Chen Hongguang replaced Chen Jiaqiu. The Shanghai team after winning the football championship (Wang Kai photo)

After the touch, Guangdong still besieged the Shanghai goal. The iron gate blocked left and right, made four dive saves, and caught the ball seven times, so that the Guangdong army could not cross the forbidden zone. The performance was unprecedented. The applause in the whole game was electric and the limelight was extremely great.

Shanghai Team Triumphs in Three Categories: Chairman Jin Ge Moves to Shanghai 191

After ten minutes, Guangdong brave general Mai Su was injured beside the Shanghai goal and fell to the ground. After being rescued off the field, Zhu Guolun replaced him, and Guangdong's momentum was weakened. Shanghai took the opportunity to rise up. Li Chen led the children straight to the Guangdong side, with the force of pushing mountains and overturning seas, unstoppable. Li Tiansheng, with his extremely rich experience and the cleanest foot, found it difficult to cope with the difficult situation. By the 26th minute, Li Yichen passed the ball to Sun Jinshun. Sun caught up and the Guangdong goalkeeper rushed out to save the ball but failed to catch it, and the ball went lightly into the net, opening the scoring. The whole audience cheered, and the Shanghai team was overjoyed and its momentum was even stronger. Guangdong tried hard to counterattack, but ultimately failed. At 30 minutes, Zhong Yongsen got the ball and sprinted, urgently using a long ball to pass to Wan Xianghua. Wan passed it to Sun Jinshun, the goalkeeper was flustered and hit another ball, making it 2-0. Guangdong's momentum was gone, and it was impossible to recover. By the 37th minute, Li Yichen got another ball. Afterwards, Guangdong averted dangerous goals. In the second half, 3-0, Shanghai won. Shanghai thus won this football championship, and President Lin of the National Government's glorious Jin Ge moved to the Shanghai army to maintain the next conference.

Shanghai is Average in Talent: Guangdong's Failure Lies in the Goalkeeper 192

As for the skills of the two teams, the Guangdong team's connection and passing of the five forwards, and their head

superiority, is indeed not something that the Shanghai team can match. Defender Li Tiansheng, with his commanding presence, is also not to be underestimated. Their weakness lies in the slightly weaker center back line, and the goalkeeper is not good. The goalkeeper cannot even talk about technique. Guangdong's two football mistakes were both due to the goalkeeper. Shanghai's team is average in talent. The five forwards, under the close supervision of the Guangdong army, have an extremely high profile. In particular, Wan Xianghua met Li Tiansheng, which was truly a dose of medicine, unable to move at all. The center and interior defenders are very competent. Sun and Li are both ministers of rescue. Speaking of the iron gate, Zhou's contribution in this game is of course the greatest. The goalkeeping technique has become miraculous, otherwise they would have lost at least three or five goals. Shanxi Wins Women's Tennis Championship: Complete Victory Over Sichuan in Three Sets; Wang Sisters Beat the World 194

Nanjing, 19th. The women's tennis championship final was held at 9:00 AM on the 19th. Wang Chunwei (Jin) (4-6 7-5 6-3) Li Yupin (Sichuan)

Sichuan gave up the doubles

▲ Wang Chunjing Steadily Takes Bao Dajing Shanxi tennis sisters, Wang Chunjing and Chunwei, have shown their prowess since the first two games. Wang Chunjing's net is appropriate, and the long shot is also good. At the beginning of the first singles, he killed three levels, and in the fourth game, Bao Dajing took advantage of the fast ball to turn the game around, making it 3-1. Wang Chunjing saw that the momentum was very fierce, and used the method of attacking from afar to make Master Bao suffer, and won the first set 6-3. In the second set, both sides cheered up, and the Sichuan generals tried to catch up after losing the first set. The battle was quite exciting, from each one to each three. The competition was the most intense. In the next game, Jin Wang won by a long shot, but was soon caught up by the Sichuan generals to a tie. Bao Dajing was very angry, but Jin Wang used the bottom line draw, which was smooth and flawless, and it was ultimately difficult to succeed. At 6-6, Wang Chunjing suddenly rose and won two consecutive games, winning the second set 8-6.

▲ Wang Chunwei Wins Li Yupin with Wisdom In the second singles, Jin Wang Chunwei played against Chuan Li Yupin. At the beginning of the game, the strength of the two armies was balanced. Li was rich in experience, and Wang was beneficial to intelligence. It can be said that they were well-matched. Chuan general served well, and Wang was struggling to parry. Chuan Li took the lead by 6-4 and won the first set. The Shanxi lady was not willing to be outdone. In the second set, she took the lead. Li Yupin was calm and used the art of deceiving the enemy to make Wang run. Wang was young and fat and not good at running, but gradually became spirited and tried his best to save the almost-lost situation, and achieved a singles record of 7-5, which was quite dangerous. The third set was the lifeline of the whole game, which was contested by military strategists. Miss Wang came up with a plan in her mind and won two consecutive games with a slip. Li Yupin saw that the situation was not good, and also used ingenious tactics to return the color. Slippery won one game. Struggling like this for a long time, each did not forcefully kill, but focused on defending. Only Jin Wang never easily let go when the opportunity came. Seizing the opportunity, the third set was won by a score of 6-3, and Shanxi won this women's tennis championship.

Shanghai Tennis Player Qiu Feihai

Flying Hailike Baohua 197

▲ Momentary Brilliance: In the first set, Qiu served first and immediately won the first game. Lin returned the favor in the same way, tying the score at one apiece. Lin then won two consecutive games, taking a commanding lead of 3-1. Qiu quickly caught up, winning his serve, but Lin won two more games with a slice, leading 5-3. Qiu refused to be outdone, winning back two games, tying the score at 5-5. Qiu's serve failed, putting him at a disadvantage at 5-6. In the next game, Qiu gave away the first set with three errors.

▲ Ultimately Extraordinary: Starting the second set, Qiu was determined and launched a vigorous counterattack. As expected, everything went smoothly, with overwhelming momentum. Although Lin tried his best to resist, he was ultimately ineffective, losing game after game, with Qiu winning five straight. In the final game, Lin made a kill shot, but Qiu still won the set with a clean sweep.

▲ Coming from Behind: After a crushing defeat in the previous set, Lin knew that he couldn't win by force alone. So, at the beginning of the third set, he applied great pressure, feinting attacks to the east and west, and winning two consecutive games with slices.

Seeing the fierce momentum, Qiu realized that only a clever approach would work. As expected, he achieved initial success and quick victory, also using slices to retaliate and tying the score at 2-2. Afterwards, both players lost their serves until they reached a 4-4 tie. In the ninth game, Qiu's serve unexpectedly turned the tide and he won, leading 5-4. The next game was a matter of life and death, with each player carefully defending. But Lin's serve was more reliable, giving him an absolute advantage at 40-15. However, Qiu also knew the importance of this game and refused to give up easily, resolutely fighting back. Lin Baohua, a tennis player from Sichuan,

tied the score and then tied it several more times. Lin ultimately failed again with a self-inflicted error. Qiu then came from behind to win with a score of two sets to one, showing his prowess.

▲ Final Victory: After a short break, the battle resumed. By this time, both players were exhausted. Lin, having lost two sets in a row, showed signs of anxiety and made hurried movements, leading to numerous errors. Qiu, on the other hand, remained unusually calm and composed, revealing nothing. Although his calf muscles cramped up at one point, he continued to advance bravely and attack. At the beginning of the set, Qiu took a commanding lead of 4-0. Although Lin attempted to counterattack and win back two games, the overall situation was hopeless. In the end, Lin made another self-inflicted error, losing the fourth set 6-3. In total, Qiu won the final victory with a score of three sets to one.

▲ A Matter of Luck: Looking at the players' skills, each had their strengths and weaknesses, making it difficult to determine who was better. Lin's serve was sharp and swift, and his net play was ingenious. Qiu's reach was long and powerful, and his play was steady and reliable. But Lin's biggest flaw was his inability to control his temper. This was the reason for his defeat on the 19th. In short, the two players were evenly matched in skill, and both were top tennis players in our country. Victory or defeat was due to luck, good or bad.

Wen Zheng Defeats Yao Bin 198

▲ Improved Technique: Qian Yaobin, a former Shanghai junior player representing Sichuan, has improved a lot. His forehand shots are extremely powerful. Wang Wenzheng had a difficult time dealing with them. Therefore, the competition in each set was close and hard to separate. The first set lasted as long as twenty-two games before a winner was decided. From beginning to end, they followed each other closely, with each winning a game in turn, neither giving up slightly. Qian played with ease, repeatedly achieving remarkable feats of skill. Wang made many self-inflicted errors, making it difficult for him to win. Wang took the lead due to his advantage in serving. After the score was tied at 10-10, Wang finally won 12-10, but it was a hard-fought victory. Wang made many errors, while Qian's backhand shots were even more successful, winning the second set 6-2.

▲ Ultimately Victorious: After each winning one set, the two sides competed even more fiercely. The third set was again difficult to decide. In the struggle, Wang took the lead 4-1, and the situation was extremely favorable. After Qian won his serve, Wang repeatedly made self-inflicted errors, while Qian's brilliance was fully revealed. In an instant, the score was tied at 5-5. Wang won his serve, and Qian returned the favor, making it 6-6 again. Wang then tightened his grip and won two consecutive games, winning the fourth set 8-6. Qian was already at the end of his strength, and his shots had no confidence. When his shots touched the net and fell short, Wang won five games in one breath, but then carelessly gave away one game and ended with 6-1.

Wu Tiecheng and Chen Lifu Hosted a Banquet for Northeastern Athletes Yesterday 200

(Nanjing, Central News Agency, 19th) Wu Tiecheng and Chen Lifu, members of the Central Committee, have always been very concerned about the Northeast issue and have a deep friendship with people from the Northeast. At 5:30 pm on the 19th, they invited more than 90 people, including team leaders of the Northeast athletes, as well as representatives of the Northeast people residing in Beijing, to a banquet at the Central Hotel. Wu gave a speech, briefly saying that since the fall of the Northeast, the Northeastern compatriots have been scattered in all directions. Fortunately, the National Games are being held in Beijing, and the Northeastern athletes are actively participating in performance sports, promoting the national spirit, which is commendable. He specially invited everyone to have a good time. The invasion of our Northeast by a strong neighbor is the prelude to the destruction of China. Saving the Northeast is saving China. We can only work hard to improve ourselves and strive to save the country. He proposed a toast, wishing everyone good health. Chen then gave a speech, briefly saying that the participation of the Northeastern athletes in the National Games actually shows that although our land has fallen into enemy hands, the people's politics are still unified and complete. We should pay attention to physical, intellectual, and moral education in the future to save the country. He hoped that everyone would work hard. Wang Zhuoran, acting president of Northeastern University, delivered a reply speech, first expressing his gratitude, and then stating five hopes: (1) Provide relief to Northeastern refugees; (2) Provide additional funding to schools that accommodate Northeastern students to support their cultivation; (3) Resettle unemployed compatriots from the Northeast; (4) Provide relief to the families of the righteous army; (5) Hope that the central government has a comprehensive plan for the revitalization of the Northeast, and so on. Finally, everyone shouted slogans such as "Long live the Northeast," "Long live the Kuomintang," and "Long live the Republic of China" and dispersed.

Hebei Wins Men's Basketball Championship ▲ Result: 49-30 Victory over Shanghai ▲ Hebei's Five Players are Lively and Extraordinary ▲ Shanghai is Disoriented, Showing Vigor in the Second Half 201

(Nanjing, 19th) In the men's basketball competition, Hebei defeated Shanghai 49-30 to win the championship. Hebei's teamwork was extremely skillful, and guard Zhang Jingde was able to attack and defend, especially agile. Shanghai lost both its home advantage and its unity, far less brave and skilled than when in Shanghai. The inability of the forwards to defend was the biggest reason for their defeat. At the end of the first half, Hebei led 18-10. At the beginning of the second half, Chen Xianglong came on for Shanghai, and the situation changed dramatically, closely following Hebei, with the score at 18-20, Hebei only leading by two points. But in an instant, Hebei regained momentum, and Yu Jingxiao repeatedly made remarkable contributions. In the end, Hebei 49, Shanghai 30. Hebei won the basketball championship of the Second National Games.

Men's Basketball Championship Hebei Team

▲ Each Team Has Its Own Talents: Hebei has Tang Baokun's assistance, Yu Jingxiao's bravery, and Zhang Jingde's superb skills. Shanghai has Lu Zhongen's strategy, Feng Nianhua's speed, and Wu Guolin's wonderful shooting. Each has its own strengths. The competition was fierce. It is a pity that the refereeing was not perfect, which was a slight blemish. In the end, Hebei won 49-30 to win the championship. The details of the competition are summarized below.

▲ Hebei Displays Dominance: The two teams face off, each with drawn swords and cocked crossbows, preparing to fight. Song Junfu and Tong Furan, the battle begins with a fanfare. Hebei's Zhang Jingde gets the ball from Tang Baokun and strides forward. Before Wu Guolin can make a contribution, he commits a foul. Hebei gets one point from the free throw. Zhang Jingde attacks again and scores again. Wu Guolin redeems himself, making the score 3-2. Hebei makes several short passes, and Zhang Jingde seizes the flag three times. Yu Jingxiao launches an attack from the middle and also scores. Zhao Shouchang prevents Feng Nianhua from shooting under the basket, making one of two free throws. Qian Jingyong arrives belatedly. Zhang Jingde is as fast as lightning, breaking through the enemy camp four times. Zhao Shouchang launches an attack from the west, and Feng Nianhua's rescue is too violent. Hebei gets another point. Tang Baokun fouls, and Qian Jingyong safely benefits.

▲ Shanghai Sees the Situation Deteriorating: and calls a timeout. With the momentum still strong, the battle resumes. Qian Jingyong gets a pass from Feng Nianhua on the baseline and breaks through the basket. Shanghai launches a second counterattack, but Feng Nianhua misses an opportunity under the basket. Tang Baokun does not return to defend but hides under the basket. Zhao Shouchang sees an opportunity and passes the ball from afar. Tang Baokun profits. Wu Guolin displays his skills, breaking straight in. Qian Jingyong loses his defense. Zhang Jingbao, like a horse freed from its reins, gets a pass from Tang Baokun on the sideline, raises his hand and scores two more points. Qian Jingyong is determined to retaliate, dribbling forward. Zhang Jingbao refuses to give up, obstructing him and committing a foul. Lu Zhongen turns around and shoots out, and Qian Jingyong shoots in the air, surprisingly hitting the target. Hebei's forwards make connecting advances. Wu Guoxia defends back and forth. Lu Zhongen loses sight of one while attending to the other. Shen Yugong cleverly steals a ball. Feng Nianhua gets a ball from Sun Baoqing and goes straight under the basket. Zhang Jingde is unwilling to give up and pushes hard. Jian Qin Tong Furan hesitates for a long time and judges it as a foul, but neither side gains anything. At the end of the first half, Hebei 16, Shanghai 10.

▲ Shanghai's Efforts Fall Short: Changing sides to fight again, Qian Jingyong moves slowly, and Zhang Jingde scores two points first. Veteran Chen Xianglong cannot help but be furious and puts on his armor and goes into battle. As expected, the momentum is greatly enhanced. Feng Nianhua skillfully avoids Zhao Shouchang and makes a hit. Instantly he's as slippery as a loach and incomparably lively. Zhen Xianglong jumps down a ball, and Feng Nianhua succeeds in one fell swoop. Liu Zhenyuan replaces Shen Yugong. He immediately commits a foul as soon as he comes on. ▲ Hebei Suffers a Setback: Shanghai is about to go to another level and turn defeat into victory. Unexpectedly, Zhang Jingde becomes active again and scores two points. The Shanghai team attacks repeatedly, and the referee is particularly sensitive, accumulating fouls. Yu Jingxiao makes a free throw, and Tang Baokun follows up with a ball. Lu Zhongen, with the skills of a great general, snatches back two points from the crowd. Yu Jingxiao launches an attack from the middle, but Chen Xianglong's block is ineffective. Tang Baokun receives Yu Jingxiao's ball and throws it in the air, surprisingly getting a stroke of good luck and scoring another point. Chen Xianglong and Feng Nianhua recover three balls from two directions. However, Tang Baokun is always a lucky general, throwing once and throwing twice, and again seeing success. Qian Jingyong enters the field again, but it does not make up for the overall situation. Only Hebei's men are seen running back and forth, full of energy. Sun Baoqing causes Zhang Jingde to foul, but the free throw is not made. It turns out to be a blessing in disguise and gets two points instead. Zhang Jingde fouls four times, but the record does not notice, and he gets four more points. Hebei then wins Shanghai 49-20.

▲ Discussing Both Sides' Skills: Hebei and Lu are all from Hebei, and their teamwork is especially commendable. Zhang Jingde's defense and attack are both well-balanced. Tang Baokun's assistance is effective. He is indeed a head above the rest. The Shanghai team is used to fighting indoors, and the ball is not what they are used to, so they are at a disadvantage in terms of terrain. In addition, Qian Jingyong's defense is ineffective, making it difficult for the defenders to defend. Lu Zhongen is good at guarding, although his throws are very inaccurate. Shen Yugong has also not been able to achieve success. In terms of skill, Hebei's teamwork is better.

Guangdong Wins Baseball Championship 202

▲ Result: 4-1 Victory over Hebei

Guangdong's Pitcher Gao Wanen Has Excellent Skills

Match Resumed in the Fourth Inning After Guangdong Players Used Force to Mediate

(Nanjing, 19th) In the men's baseball final, Guangdong played against Hebei. Guangdong attacked first, and the situation was tense. There were no records in the first five innings. In the top of the sixth inning, Guangdong's Wu Shunde got a hit. In addition, Hebei's fielder made a decisive error, and Guangdong scored three points in a row. Hebei resisted forcefully, and the momentum was great. With the bases loaded, Guangdong's defense was tight. Only Liang Ruilin got one point. In the ninth inning, Guangdong added another point. As a result, Guangdong won 4-1 to win the championship. Guangdong's pitcher Gao Wanen has excellent skills, leaving Hebei with no way to survive. In the top of the fourth inning, Guangdong and Hebei players used force. The entire team surrounded and beat Hebei's first baseman Feng Daoyuan. After the referee and Hebei officials tried their best to mediate, the game continued. After the game, Hebei wanted to retaliate and asked the military police not to interfere. The military police did not agree and defended very strictly, so no trouble occurred.

▲ Lin Jinyou's Arm of Iron: Guangdong's pitcher Lin Jinyou was born with an arm of iron and has trained his entire arm. His fingers have strong control, and the ball's arc is sufficient, leaving Hebei with no way to survive. In the nine innings, Hebei had a total of nine players who struck out, and he only let one walk. After Guangdong scored two points in the sixth inning, Hebei tried to counterattack. With the bases loaded, Jin Yun used his full strength and showed his wonderful pitches. Sure enough, he was miraculous, and Hebei only got one point. As a result, Guangdong won 4-1 to win the championship.

▲ No Success in the First Three Innings: Guangdong attacked first. At the beginning, the first three were killed and did not get on base. The same was true for Hebei. The first inning passed peacefully. Two Guangdong players struck out in succession. Cheng Guanjie got a hit, but Huang Yunbao's high ball went out of bounds, and they did not gain anything. Hebei was trapped by the strict defense, and three players struck out in succession. The second inning was still without a record. In the third inning, after two Guangdong players were out, Mao Lianrong took advantage of an error at first base to get on base, and then advanced to third base. The situation suddenly became tense, but Wu Shunde hit a high ball, and the shortstop made a wonderful backhand catch. Guangdong still did not score. Hebei's Luo Zongqiang used his strength, but each struck out, and the overall situation was gone. In the first three innings, both sides' formations were tight, with no gaps to take advantage of.

▲ Full-Scale Fight with Fierce Momentum: A dispute suddenly arose in the fourth inning. Guangdong's Gao Hansi hit the ball, and the third baseman intercepted it and threw it to first base. The ball arrived first, but Gao still rushed to first base with all his might, hitting Hebei's first baseman Feng Daoyuan. Feng scolded him, but Gao, without distinguishing right from wrong, punched him. Other Guangdong players also swarmed up and launched a general attack on Feng. The situation was serious and terrible for a time. Fortunately, other Hebei players understood the importance of the situation and did not join the battle. The referees and others tried their best to mediate, and the game was able to continue.

The game then ended, and Guangdong won the championship with a score of 4-1. Guangdong had a total of five hits, and Hebei only had two. Swimming Quick Records 204

▲ Women's 200m Backstroke (Nanjing, 19th) In the women's 200m backstroke final, there were a total of five participants. At 15 meters, Shi Ruisheng took the lead, but after 50 meters, she was overtaken by Yang Xiuqiong. At 100 meters, she was overtaken by Yang Xiuzhen. At 150 meters, she was overtaken by Lin Duli. Yang Xiuqiong led all the way to the finish line after 50 meters, winning by about 10 meters over second place. The Yang sisters took the top two spots. The first place, Xiuqiong, had a time of 3 minutes and 4 seconds.

▲ Men's 100m Freestyle In the 100m freestyle final, there were a total of eight participants. At the start, the competition was extremely fierce. After 40 meters, Chen Zhenxing took the lead, leading by one meter. When turning at 50 meters, Chen was also the fastest, followed by Chen Qisong, Wang Xiushan, and Shi Xingzhi, each with a difference of no more than half a meter. Chen Zhenxing ultimately won first place, swimming the entire course with one breath. Chen's time was 1 minute and 6.4 seconds, failing to break the national record. The first, second, and third places were all taken by Guangdong Province. The young Shi Xingzhi from Liaoning was selected for fourth place.

▲ Men's 200m Backstroke There were a total of eight participants. In the first 50 meters, the strength of each competitor was evenly matched, and only then could the differences be seen. When turning at 50 meters, Wang Yaomin first surpassed, but at 100 meters, Guo Zhenheng suppressed Wang and took the lead. At this time, Dong Chun from Hebei suddenly made rapid progress and ran alongside Guo Zhenheng, but when reaching the finish line, he was ultimately defeated by Guo Zhenheng by two meters. Guo's time was 3 minutes and 5.2 seconds, breaking the national record of 3 minutes and 28 seconds.

▲ Women's 100m Freestyle In the women's 100m freestyle final, there were originally six people, but He Wenya from Qingdao and Shi Ruisheng from Liaoning withdrew. Only four people attended: Yang Xiuqiong, Yang Xiuzhen, Chen Huanqiong, and Chen Yuhui. At the start, Yang Xiuqiong was the fastest, leading the way like a mermaid. Yang's graceful posture surprised the audience, who scrambled to see the standard beauty. As a result, Yang won by five meters over Chen Huanqiong in second place, Chen Yuhui in third place, and Yang Xiuzhen in fourth place. The time was 1 minute and 29.9 seconds.

▲ Women's 200m Relay In the women's 200m relay final, there were a total of three teams participating: Hong Kong, Guangdong, and Qingdao. Hong Kong had the most strength, so they led the way from beginning to end. When reaching the finish line, they were more than 20 meters ahead of the second-place Guangdong team. The time was 2 minutes and 49 seconds. The list of the top three teams is as follows: (1) Shanghai Team: Liu Guizhen, Yang Xiuzhen, Liang Yongxian, Yang Xiuqiong; (2) Guangdong Team: Chen Tianhui, Yuan Peizhang, Chen Huanqiong; (3) Qingdao Team: He Wenjing, Wu Yuzhen, He Wenjin, He Wenya. The time was 2 minutes and 49 seconds.

▲ Exhibition Swimming To increase interest after the end, Shi Xinglong specially performed "Overlord Crossing the River" individually. Shi held his hands over his head and swam from the north end of the pool

to the south end. He then performed a mixed relay, with participants including two teams from Guangdong, one team from Hong Kong, one team from Shanghai, and one guest team. As a result, Guangdong won. Finally, the guests and athletes performed fancy diving. The mixed relay was 150 meters, with the first 50 meters backstroke, the second 50 meters breaststroke, and the third 50 meters freestyle.

Women's Volleyball

Shanghai Wins Women's Volleyball Championship Defeats Peiping Three to One Strong Opponents Hong Kong and Guangdong Eliminated During Preliminary Rounds Shanghai's Championship Undisputed 208

(Nanking, 19th dispatch) The women's volleyball finals were held at 3 PM on the 19th.

Shanghai played against Peiping. Shanghai's lineup was exceptionally well-organized, having initially defeated Jiangxi, then Fujian, and followed with three victories over Lingnan. Their momentum was magnificent. In the championship, the strength of South China was originally quite formidable, but during the three-match week, Hong Kong and Guangdong were simultaneously eliminated. Facing Peiping in the final round, the championship was within grasp, leaving no doubt. At 2:30 PM, the referee Wu Bangwei arrived leisurely carrying the ball. Subsequently, the Shanghai team, dressed uniformly and known for their spirited nature, also arrived from the front lines, awaiting the Peiping team's entrance to begin the battle.

Preemptive Strike with Imposing Demeanor 209

Shanghai's Xiao Jieying took the initiative, displaying her fierce power, willing to die blocking and spiking against the Peiping team. Peiping scored three points on each serve. Guan Liuzhu's passing and setting were skillful, and Xue Zhijie's spiking was eager. The front row of three players desperately blocked. The battle was intense. The Peiping team, seeing the fierce and invincible opponents, became confused and lost six consecutive points. After switching sides, Qian Shuyi served consecutively, scoring until fifteen points when the ball was intercepted by the Peiping team. From then on, the lead alternated. The "Black Whirlwind" Xue Zhijie truly displayed the demeanor of a great general, serving three consecutive balls that landed in the corner, impossible to save. Peiping then lost the first set.

Helpless and Unable to Resist 210

In the second set, Peiping, seeing Shanghai's rampant performance, felt greatly ashamed. The three front players were sluggish and unable to spike effectively. They were unable to attack the enemy or defend the net, leading to a complete collapse. They simply awaited the referee's decision, lacking any ability to resist. The score of this set was 21 to 5, with Shanghai winning.

Carelessness Leads to Loss, Blame Lies with Themselves 211

In the third set, Peiping changed personnel and launched a counterattack. Shanghai, arrogant due to their victories, played without brilliance. As expected, arrogance leads to defeat. In a short time, the saying was proven. In the first half of the set, Shanghai trailed 9 to 11. After switching sides, Shanghai turned it around to 17 to 11. Shanghai only needed one more point to end the set, but they became complacent and careless in facing their opponents. Unexpectedly, the front row failed to block, losing a point, and Peiping served again. At the same time, two hard spikes went out of bounds. At this point, Peiping's score took the lead at 21 to 20. Finally, repeated net fouls occurred, eagerness to win led to consecutive self-inflicted losses, resulting in a 25 to 23 defeat to Peiping.

Redoubling Efforts Brings Success 212

In the fourth set, rain drizzled. The Shanghai ladies, knowing their mistake in the previous set, didn't hesitate to correct it, redoubling their efforts, and their attitude became even more calm and composed. Wang Xuehua's serves were like continuous mortar fire, completed in one go. The Peiping ladies were perpetually under bombardment, conceding as many as twelve consecutive points. The Peiping team truly appeared like survivors of a disaster. Wang Xuehua's arm was nearly broken. Subsequently, Peiping's Li Wushan passed the ball to the front row, but their light cuts and spikes made no progress. The set ended at 21 to 9, with the Shanghai women overjoyed, winning the championship.
